   8. Scaffold the Unit Test. You MUST calculate the exact AABB of the loaded geometry and mathematically frame the
   `ArcballCamera` to fit this AABB.
   9. **Verification Logging (CRITICAL):** You must print the decoded ECEF coordinates and the local ENU bounding box
   to `executor_console.log` so the Architect can verify the *correct* spatial location was loaded.
   10. **Hardware Proof (CRITICAL):** Integrate `GL_SAMPLES_PASSED` occlusion queries around the draw calls. Print the
   exact number of pixels rendered to the log.

   **Phase 3: DOD & Precision Hardening (Make It Fast)**
   11. Refactor memory: Integrate the lock-free linear arena allocator (`AliceMemory::LinearArena`) using `std::atomic`
   for async decoding.
   12. Refactor shaders: Build a Relative-To-Eye (RTE) split-double precision pipeline.

   **DIRECTIVE:**
   Act as the Orchestrator. Read `.agents/architect.md` and `.agents/executor.md`. Inject the **AGENT CONTEXT PAYLOAD**
   into both the Executor's and Architect's prompts. Pass the GOAL and MASTER PLAN to the Executor and instruct it to

   exact number of pixels rendered to the log.

   for async decoding.
   12. Refactor shaders: Build a Relative-To-Eye (RTE) split-double precision pipeline.

   subsystem. We are strictly following a 3-Phase Crucible approach: Prototype, Verify, Optimize.

   **GOAL:** Stream, decode, and properly visualize a 500m x 500m sector of Central London (St Paul's Cathedral) from
   Cesium ION.

   **AGENT CONTEXT PAYLOAD:** * Architectural constraints: You MUST read `/docs/Geospatial Engine & Agent
   Orchestration.md` before generating or reviewing code. It contains mandatory C++ APIs (`Math::denu_matrix`,
   `AliceMemory::LinearArena`).
   * Legacy Code Guardrail: You may review `/docs/code_snippets/` strictly to understand the framework's API. **DO
   NOT** attempt to patch or reuse the legacy `TilesetLoader.h` or `TilesetTest.h`. You must write clean, DOD-compliant
   code from scratch.
   * Authentication: Extract Cesium ION keys from `API_KEYS.txt` (prefix: `CESIUM_ION_KEYS = "..."`).
   * Test Protocols: Strict adherence to `executor_SOP.md` is mandatory.

   **MASTER PLAN:**

   **Phase 1: Network Proof-of-Life (Make It Work)**
   1. Parse `API_KEYS.txt` for the auth token.
   2. Implement a `libcurl` network loop using `Alice::Network::Fetch` (ensuring `CURLOPT_FOLLOWLOCATION` and
   exponential backoff for 429/503 errors).
   3. Request the 3D Tiles for the St Paul's Cathedral sector (Asset ID: 96188).
   4. Serialize and save the downloaded binary tile payloads directly to `artifacts/test_tiles/` for independent human
   inspection.
   5. THE LOOP MUST NOT HALT HERE. Proceed immediately to Phase 2.

   **Phase 2: Mathematical Prototype & Verification (Make It Right)**
   6. Parse the magic bytes of the local artifacts (`b3dm`/`glTF`).
   7. Implement 64-bit ECEF-to-ENU coordinate transformations (`Math::denu_matrix`).
   8. Scaffold the Unit Test. You MUST calculate the exact AABB of the loaded geometry and mathematically frame the
   `ArcballCamera` to fit this AABB.
   9. **Verification Logging (CRITICAL):** You must print the decoded ECEF coordinates and the local ENU bounding box
   to `executor_console.log` so the Architect can verify the *correct* spatial location was loaded.
   10. **Hardware Proof (CRITICAL):** Integrate `GL_SAMPLES_PASSED` occlusion queries around the draw calls. Print the
   exact number of pixels rendered to the log.

   **Phase 3: DOD & Precision Hardening (Make It Fast)**
   11. Refactor memory: Integrate the lock-free linear arena allocator (`AliceMemory::LinearArena`) using `std::atomic`
   for async decoding.
   12. Refactor shaders: Build a Relative-To-Eye (RTE) split-double precision pipeline.
